	</div><div class="wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-12"><div class="vc_column-inner"><div class="wpb_wrapper">
	<div class="wpb_text_column wpb_content_element " >
		<div class="wpb_wrapper">
			<h1 style="text-align: center;">Welcome to Encircle</h1>
<h2 style="text-align: center;">Connect. Transform. Enrich.</h2>
<p><img decoding="async" class="aligncenter wp-image-10480" title="Encircle Logo 2023" src="https://encircle.org.au/wp-content/uploads/2023/05/Encircle-Logo-2023.png" alt="Encircle Logo 2023" width="200" height="227" /></p>

		</div>
	</div>
</div></div></div></div><div class="vc_row-full-width vc_clearfix"></div><div data-vc-full-width="true" data-vc-full-width-init="false" class="vc_row wpb_row vc_row-fluid whiterow standard vc_custom_1601595618320 vc_row-has-fill"><div class="wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-12"><div class="vc_column-inner vc_custom_1497398204496"><div class="wpb_wrapper">
	<div class="wpb_text_column wpb_content_element  vc_custom_1669079420247" >
		<div class="wpb_wrapper">
			<h2 style="text-align: center;">Encircle: Connect. Transform. Enrich.</h2>

		</div>
	</div>
</div></div></div></div><div class="vc_row-full-width vc_clearfix"></div><div data-vc-full-width="true" data-vc-full-width-init="false" class="vc_row wpb_row vc_row-fluid whiterow vc_custom_1601595465365 vc_row-has-fill vc_column-gap-15"><div class="wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-6"><div class="vc_column-inner vc_custom_1497399277509"><div class="wpb_wrapper">
	<div class="wpb_text_column wpb_content_element  vc_custom_1601595541682 white" >
		<div class="wpb_wrapper">
			<h5>Who we are</h5>
<p><strong>We are a not for profit community owned and operated organisation for individuals and families in the northern suburbs of Brisbane.</strong></p>
<p>We can help you access a range of diverse programs including a confidential interview with the Intake and Response team to assess your individual or family support needs.</p>

		</div>
	</div>
</div></div></div><div class="wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-6"><div class="vc_column-inner vc_custom_1497399269814"><div class="wpb_wrapper">
	<div class="wpb_text_column wpb_content_element  vc_custom_1601595536698 white" >
		<div class="wpb_wrapper">
			<h5>Volunteer with us!</h5>
<p>With around 200 volunteers actively giving their time at the Pine Rivers Neighbourhood Centre, volunteering plays an integral role in the services we deliver.</p>

		</div>
	</div>

	<div class="wpb_text_column wpb_content_element  vc_custom_1669259090847" >
		<div class="wpb_wrapper">
			<h2 class="frontp" style="text-align: center;">Call us today on <a href="tel:0738890063">07 3889 0063</a> or <a href="/contact/">email us here</a></h2>
<h6><a href="https://encircle.org.au/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/Pine-Rivers-Community-Legal-Service-in-the-Moreton-Bay-Region-extended-services.pdf" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Pine Rivers Community Legal Service extension of legal assistance services in the Moreton Bay region: View the Fact Sheet here</a>.</h6>

		</div>

</div></div></div></div></div><div class="vc_row wpb_row vc_row-fluid"><div class="wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-6 vc_col-md-3"><div class="vc_column-inner"><div class="wpb_wrapper"><div class="vc_icon_element vc_icon_element-outer vc_icon_element-align-center"><div class="vc_icon_element-inner vc_icon_element-color-custom vc_icon_element-size-md vc_icon_element-style- vc_icon_element-background-color-grey" ><span class="vc_icon_element-icon fas fa-balance-scale" style="color:#5faf46 !important"></span><a class="vc_icon_element-link" href="https://encircle.org.au/pine-rivers-community-legal-service/" title="" target="_self"></a></div></div>
	<div class="wpb_text_column wpb_content_element " >
		<div class="wpb_wrapper">
			<h6 style="text-align: center;"><a href="https://encircle.org.au/pine-rivers-community-legal-service/">Community Legal Service</a></h6>
<p style="text-align: center;">Get help now. You can Consult a Solicitor. Legal help is available face to face or over the telephone.</p>

<script class="tribe-events-breakpoints">
	(function() {
		var completed = false;

		function initBreakpoints() {
			if ( completed ) {
				// This was fired already and completed no need to attach to the event listener.
				document.removeEventListener( 'DOMContentLoaded', initBreakpoints );
				return;
			}

			if ( 'undefined' === typeof window.tribe ) {
				return;
			}

			if ( 'undefined' === typeof window.tribe.filterBar ) {
				return;
			}

			if ( 'undefined' === typeof window.tribe.filterBar.filterBarState ) {
				return;
			}

			if ( 'function' !== typeof (window.tribe.filterBar.filterBarState.setup) ) {
				return;
			}

			var container = document.querySelectorAll( '[data-view-breakpoint-pointer="13803ab7-69b8-48da-9356-ca11c83b50ee"]' );

			if ( ! container ) {
				return;
			}

			window.tribe.filterBar.filterBarState.setup( container );
			completed = true;
			// This was fired already and completed no need to attach to the event listener.
			document.removeEventListener( 'DOMContentLoaded', initBreakpoints );
		}

		// Try to init the breakpoints right away.
		initBreakpoints();
		document.addEventListener( 'DOMContentLoaded', initBreakpoints );
	})();
</script>

	( function () {
		var completed = false;

		function initBreakpoints() {
			if ( completed ) {
				// This was fired already and completed no need to attach to the event listener.
				document.removeEventListener( 'DOMContentLoaded', initBreakpoints );
				return;
			}

			if ( 'undefined' === typeof window.tribe ) {
				return;
			}

			if ( 'undefined' === typeof window.tribe.events ) {
				return;
			}

			if ( 'undefined' === typeof window.tribe.events.views ) {
				return;
			}

			if ( 'undefined' === typeof window.tribe.events.views.breakpoints ) {
				return;
			}

			if ( 'function' !== typeof (window.tribe.events.views.breakpoints.setup) ) {
				return;
			}

			var container = document.querySelectorAll( '[data-view-breakpoint-pointer="13803ab7-69b8-48da-9356-ca11c83b50ee"]' );
			if ( ! container ) {
				return;
			}

			window.tribe.events.views.breakpoints.setup( container );
			completed = true;
			// This was fired already and completed no need to attach to the event listener.
			document.removeEventListener( 'DOMContentLoaded', initBreakpoints );
		}

		// Try to init the breakpoints right away.
		initBreakpoints();
		document.addEventListener( 'DOMContentLoaded', initBreakpoints );
	})();
</script>

<p><b>From 1 December 2023 Encircle Community Services will no longer be managing halls. Please go to </b><a href="https://www.moretonbay.qld.gov.au/Services/Sport-Recreation/Halls" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Halls and meeting rooms &#8211; City of Moreton Bay</a> <b>for bookings or for more information.</b></p>

<script></script><script type="text/javascript">
function tw_2_next_index( index, increment ) {
	if ( ! increment ) {
		index++;
	}

	if ( null == index || isNaN( index ) || index >= 20 ) {
		index = 0;
	}

	jQuery.cookie('rotatePerPage2', index, { path: '/' });

	return index;
}

var cnt_tw_2 = 0;

jQuery(document).ready( function() {
cnt_tw_2 = jQuery.cookie('rotatePerPage2');
cnt_tw_2 = tw_2_next_index( cnt_tw_2, true );
});
</script><script type="text/javascript">
var tw_2 = null;

jQuery(document).ready(function() {
	/*added to check the screensize to enable swipe effect for the bxslider*/
	jQuery(window).on("resize", function (e) {
		checkScreenSize();
	});
	checkScreenSize()
	 /*custom function to process swipe effect*/
	 function checkScreenSize()
	{
		var newWindowWidth = jQuery(window).width();
		if (newWindowWidth >= 767)
		{
			tw_2 = jQuery('.testimonials-widget-testimonials2').bxSlider({
				adaptiveHeight: false,
				auto: true,
				
				autoHover: true,
				prevSelector: '.testimonials-widget-testimonials2-control',
nextSelector: '.testimonials-widget-testimonials2-control',
				mode: 'fade',
				pager: false,
				pause: 5000,
				video: false,
				slideMargin: 2,
	startSlide: cnt_tw_2,
	onSlideAfter: function( $slideElement, oldIndex, newIndex ) {
		tw_2_next_index( newIndex );
	},
					adaptiveHeightSpeed: 500,
					speed: 500,
				slideWidth: 0,
				touchEnabled:false
			});
		}
		else
		{
			tw_2 = jQuery('.testimonials-widget-testimonials2').bxSlider({
				adaptiveHeight: false,
				auto: true,
				
				autoHover: true,
				prevSelector: '.testimonials-widget-testimonials2-control',
nextSelector: '.testimonials-widget-testimonials2-control',
				mode: 'fade',
				pager: false,
				pause: 5000,
				video: false,
				slideMargin: 2,
	startSlide: cnt_tw_2,
	onSlideAfter: function( $slideElement, oldIndex, newIndex ) {
		tw_2_next_index( newIndex );
	},
					adaptiveHeightSpeed: 500,
					speed: 500,
				slideWidth: 0				
			});
		}
	}
	
});

function tw_100000_next_index( index, increment ) {
	if ( ! increment ) {
		index++;
	}

	if ( null == index || isNaN( index ) || index >= 30 ) {
		index = 0;
	}

	jQuery.cookie('rotatePerPage100000', index, { path: '/' });

	return index;
}

var cnt_tw_100000 = 0;

jQuery(document).ready( function() {
cnt_tw_100000 = jQuery.cookie('rotatePerPage100000');
cnt_tw_100000 = tw_100000_next_index( cnt_tw_100000, true );
});
